   // Daśabhūmikasūtram //	// DaSa BUmika sUtram //
   1 pramuditā nāma prathamā bhūmiḥ /	1 pramuditA nAma praTamA BUmiH /
   evaṃ mayā śrutam / ekasmin samaye bhagavān paranirmitavaśavartiṣu	evam mayA Srutam / ekasmin samaye BagavAn paranirmita vaSavartizu
   devabhuvaneṣu viharati sma acirābhisaṃbuddho dvitīye saptāhe vaśavartino	deva Buvanezu viharati sma acira aBisaMbudDaH dvitIye sapta ahe vaSavartinaH 
   devarājasya vimāne maṇiratnagarbhe prabhāsvare prāsāde mahatā	devarAjasya vimAne maNi ratna garBe praBAsvare prAsAde mahatA

   yaduta anuttarāyāṃ samyaksaṃbodhāvanyonyalokadhātusaṃnipatitaiḥ / sarvaiḥ	yat uta anuttarAyAm samyaksaMboDO= anyonya loka DAtu saMnipatitEH / sarvEH
   sarvabodhisattvajñānaviṣayagocarapratilabdhavihāribhiḥ	sarva boDisattva jQAna vizaya gocara pratilabDa vihAriBiH

   sarvajagatparipācanavinayayathākālakṣaṇādhiṣṭhānasarvakriyāsaṃdarśanakuśalaiḥ	sarva jagat paripAcana vinaya yaTA kA lakzaNa aDizWAna sarva kriyA saMdarSana kuSalEH

   kalpārthakṣetracaryāsaṃvāsibhiḥ	kalpa arTa kzetra caryA saMvAsiBiH

   sarvabodhisattvaprajñopāyaparamapāramitāprāptaiḥ	sarva boDisattva prajQA upAya parama pAramitA prAptEH

   sarvabodhisattvadhyānavimokṣasamādhisamāpatyabhijñājñānavikrīḍitābhijñāsarvakriyāsaṃdarśanakuśalaiḥ	sarva boDisattva DyAna vimokza samADi samApati aBijQA jQAna vikrIxita aBijQA sarva kriyA saMdarSana kuSalEH
   sarvabodhisattvarddhibalavaśitāprāptānabhisaṃskāracittakṣaṇasarvatathāgataparṣanmaṇḍalopasaṃkramaṇapūrvaṃgamakathāpuruṣaiḥ	sarva boDisattva RdDi bala vaSitA prApta anaBisaMskAra citta kzaNa sarva taTAgata parzan maNxala upasaMkramaNa pUrvaMgama kaTA puruzEH
   sarvatathāgatadharmacakrasaṃdhāraṇavipulabuddhapūjopasthānābhyutthitaiḥ	sarva taTAgata Darma cakra saMDAraNa vipula budDa pUjA upasTAna aByutTitEH
   sarvabodhisattvakarmasamādānasamatāprayogasarvalokadhātukāyapratibhāsaprāptaiḥ	sarva boDisattva karma sama AdAna sama tA prayoga sarva loka DAtu kAya pratiBAsa prAptEH
   sarvadharmadhātvasaṅgasvararutaghoṣānuravitasarvatryadhvāsaṅgacittajñānaviṣayaspharaṇaiḥ	sarva DarmaDAtu asaFga svara ruta Goza anuravita sarva tri aDvAsaFga citta jQAna vizaya sParaNEH
   sarvabodhisattvaguṇapratipattisuparipūrṇānabhilāpyakalpādhiṣṭhānasaṃprakāśanāparikṣīṇaguṇavarṇanirdeśakaiḥ	sarva boDisattva guNa pratipatti su paripUrNa anaBilApya kalpa aDizWAna saMprakASanA parikzINa guNa varNa nirdeSakEH
   / yadidamvajragarbheṇa ca bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / ratnagarbheṇa ca /	/ yat idam vajra garBeNa ca boDisattvena mahAsattvena / ratna garBeNa ca /

   / anāvaraṇasvaramaṇḍalamadhuranirghoṣagarbheṇa ca /	/ anAvaraNa svara maNxala maDura nirGoza garBeNa ca /

   ca / (Dbh 2) meruśrīgarbheṇa ca / sarvaguṇaviśuddhigarbheṇa ca /	ca / (DB 2) meru SrI garBeNa ca / sarva guNa viSudDi garBeNa ca /

   bodhisattvena mahāsattvena / evaṃpramukhair	boDisattvena mahAsattvena / evaMpramuKEH 
   aparimāṇāprameyāsaṃkhyeyācintyātulyāmāpyānantāparyantāsīmāprāptānabhilāpyānabhilāpyairbodhisattvairmahāsattvaiḥ	aparimANa aprameya asaMKyeya acintya atulyAm Apya anantA paryanta AsIm A prApta anaBilApya anaBilApyEH boDisattvEH mahAsattvEH
   sārdhaṃ nānābuddhakṣetrasaṃnipatitairvajragarbhabodhisattvapūrvaṃgamaiḥ //	sArDam nAnA budDa kzetra saMnipatitEH vajra garBa boDisattva pUrvaMgamEH //
   atha khalu vajragarbho bodhisattvayāṃ velāyāṃ buddhānubhāvena	aTa Kalu vajragarBaH boDisattvayAm velAyAm budDa anuBAvena

   samanantarasamāpannaśca vajragarbho bodhisattva imaṃ mahāyānaprabhāsaṃ	samanantara samApannaH ca vajragarBaH boDisattvaH imam mahAyAna praBA sam
   nāma bodhisattvasamādhim,atha tāvadeva daśasu dikṣu	nAma boDisattva samADim ,aTa tAvat eva daSasu dikzu
   daśabuddhakṣetrakoṭiparamāṇurajaḥsamānāṃ lokadhātūnāmapareṇa	daSa budDa kzetra kowi paramANu rajaH samAnAm lokaDAtUnAm apareNa

   daśasu dikṣu daśabuddhakṣetrakoṭiparamāṇurajaḥsamānāṃ lokadhātūnāmapareṇa	daSasu dikzu daSa budDa kzetra kowi paramANu rajaH samAnAm lokaDAtUnAm apareNa

   suvicitavicayamahāprajñālokakauśalyāya /	su vicita vicaya mahA prajQA loka kOSalyAya /

   (Dbh 3) ca apramāṇasmṛtibhājanatayā ca prabhāsvarādhimuktiviśodhanatayā ca	(DB 3) ca apramANa smRti BAjana tayA ca praBAsvarADi mukti viSoDana tayA ca

   etaddharmavipākena kṣāntivratamupāśrayet // 37 //	etad Darma vipAkena kzAntivratam upASrayet // 37 //
   samyakkṣāntivrataṃ dhṛtvā kṣāntibhṛtkuśalī bhavet /	samyak kzAnti vratam DRtvA kzAnti BRt kuSalI Bavet /
   tataḥ prabhākarīprāptastrayastriṃśādhipo bhavet // 38 //	tatas praBAkarI prAptaH trayastriMSa aDipaH Bavet // 38 //
   tatrasthaḥ pālayan sattvān kleśamārganivāraṇaiḥ /	tatrasTaH pAlayan sattvAn kleSa mArga nivAraNEH /
   svayaṃ kṣāntivrate sthitvā parāṃścāpi niyojayet // 39 //	svayam kzAnti vrate sTitvA parAn= ca api niyojayet // 39 //
   sattvān bodhau pratiṣṭhāpya kṣāntipāraṃgato bhavet /	sattvAn boDO pratizWApya kzAnti pAraMgataH Bavet /
   etatpuṇyavipākaiḥ sa vīryavratamupāśrayet // 40 //	etat puNya vipAkEH sa vIrya vratam upASrayet // 40 //
   samyagvīryaṃ samādhāya vīryabhṛt kuśalī bhavet /	samyak vIryam samADAya vIrya BRt kuSalI Bavet /
   tataścārciṣmatīprāptaḥ suyāmādhipatirbhavet // 41 //	tatas ca arcizmatI prAptaH suyAma aDipatiH Bavet // 41 //
   tatrasthaḥ pālayan sattvān kudṛṣṭisaṃnivāraṇaiḥ /	tatrasTaH pAlayan sattvAn kudRzwi saMnivAraNEH /
   samyagdṛṣṭau pratiṣṭhāpya bodhayitvā prayatnataḥ // 42 //	samyak dRzwO pratizWApya boDayitvA prayatnataH // 42 //
   svayaṃ vīryavrate sthitvā parāṃścāpi niyojayet /	svayam vIrya vrate sTitvA parAn= ca api niyojayet /
   sarvān bodhau pratiṣṭhāpya vīryapāraṃgato bhavet // 43 //	sarvAn boDO pratizWApya vIrya pAraMgataH Bavet // 43 //
   etatpuṇyavipākaiśca dhyānavrataṃ samāśrayet /	etat puNya vipAkEH ca DyAna vratam samASrayet /

   samyag dhyānaṃ samādhāya samādhikuśalī bhavet /	samyak DyAnam samADAya samADi kuSalI Bavet /

   tatrasthaḥ pālayan sattvān tīrthyamārganivāraṇaiḥ /	tatrasTaH pAlayan sattvAn tIrTya mArga nivAraNEH /

   etatpuṇyavipākaiśca prajñāvratamupāśrayet /	etat puNya vipAkEH ca prajQA vratam upASrayet /
   sarvamārān vinirjitya prajñābhijñasamṛddhimān // 48 //	sarvam ArAn vinirjitya prajQA aBijQa samRdDimAn // 48 //

   sa supāyavidhānena sattvān bodhau niyojayet /	sa su pAya viDAnena sattvAn boDO niyojayet /
   tato dūraṃgamāprāpto vaśavartīśvaro bhavet // 53 //	tatas dUraMgama aprAptaH vaSa varti ISvaraH Bavet // 53 //

   tatropāye svayaṃ sthitvā parāṃścāpi niyojayet /	tatra upAye svayam sTitvA parAn= ca api niyojayet /

   etatpuṇyānusāraiśca balavratamupāśrayet /	etat puNya anusArEH ca bala vratam upASrayet /

   samyagbalasamutsāhaiḥ sarvatīrthyān vinirjayet /	samyak bala samutsAhEH sarva tIrTyAn vinirjayet /
   tataḥ sādhumatīprāpto mahābrahmā bhavet kṛtī // 61 //	tatas sADu matI prAptaH mahA brahmA Bavet kRtI // 61 //
   tatrasthaḥ pālayan sattvān buddhayānopadarśanaiḥ /	tatrasTaH pAlayan sattvAn budDa yAna upadarSanEH /
   sattvāśayaparijñāne pratiṣṭhāpya prabodhayan // 62 //	sattva ASaya parijQAne pratizWApya praboDayan // 62 //
   (Dbh 108)	(DB 108)
   svayaṃ bale pratiṣṭhitvā paraṃścāpi niyojayet /	svayam bale pratizWitvA paran= ca api niyojayet /
   sarvān bodhau pratiṣṭhāpya balapāraṃgato bhavet // 63 //	sarvAn boDO pratizWApya bala pAraMgataH Bavet // 63 //

   samyag jñānaṃ samāsādya saddharmakuśalī bhavet /	samyak jQAnam samAsAdya sat Darma kuSalI Bavet /

   iti matvā bhavadbhiśca saṃbodhipadalabdhaye /	iti matvA BavadBiH ca saMboDi pada labDaye /

   tathā bodhiṃ śivāṃ prāpya caturmārān vijitya ca /	taTA boDim SivAm prApya catur mArAn vijitya ca /
   sarvān bodhau pratiṣṭhāpya nirvṛtiṃ samavāpsyatha // 70 //	sarvAn boDO pratizWApya nirvRtim samavApsyaTa // 70 //
   etatcchrutvā parijñāya caradhvaṃ bodhisādhane /	etat t SrutvA parijQAya caraDvam boDi sADane /
   nirvighnaṃ bodhimāsādya labhadhvaṃ saugatāṃ gatim // 71 //	nirviGnam boDim AsAdya laBaDvam sOgatAm gatim // 71 //

   11 parīndanāparivartaḥ /	11 parIndanA parivartaH /
   upakramaḥ /	upakramaH /
   etāstāḥ khalu punarbho jinaputrā daśa bodhisattvabhūmayaḥ samāsato	etAH tAH Kalu punarBo jinaputrAH daSa boDisattva BUmayaH samAsatas 
   nirdiṣṭāḥ sarvākāravaropetasarvajñajñānānugatā draṣṭavyāḥ / tasyāṃ	nirdizwAH sarva AkAra vara upeta sarvajQa jQAna anugatAH drazwavyAH / tasyAm
   velāyāmayaṃ trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhātuḥ ṣaḍvikāraṃ prākampat /	velAyAmayam tri sAhasra mahA sAhasraH lokaDAtuH zaz vikAram prAkampat /
   vividhāni ca puṣpāṇi viyato nyapatan / divyamānuṣyakāni ca tūryāṇi	viviDAni ca puzpANi viyataH nyapatan / divya mAnuzyakAni ca tUryANi
   saṃpravāditānyabhūvan / anumodanāśabdena ca yāvadakaniṣṭhabhuvanaṃ	saMpravAditAni aBUvan / anumodanA Sabdena ca yAvat akanizWa Buvanam
   vijñaptamabhūt //	vijQaptam aBUt //
   atha tasmin samaye bhagavāṃstān vimukticandrapramukhān sarvān	aTa tasmin samaye BagavAn= tAn vimukti candra pramuKAn sarvAn
   bodhisattvānāmantrya evamādiśat   imāmahaṃ mārṣā	boDisattvAn AmantryaH evam AdiSat  imAm aham mArzA
   asaṃkhyeyakalpakoṭīnayutaśatasahasrasamudānītāmanuttarāṃ samyaksaṃbodhiṃ	asaMKyeya kalpa kowIn ayuta Sata sahasra samudAnItAm anuttarAm samyaksaMboDim
   yuṣmākaṃ haste parindāmi anuparindāmi paramayā parindanayā / tadyūyaṃ	yuzmAkam haste parindAmi anuparindAmi paramayA parindanayA / tat yUyam
   sarve svayaṃ caivamimaṃ dharmaparyāyaṃ dhārayata, parebhyaśca vistareṇa	sarve svayam ca evam imam Darma paryAyam DArayata, pareByaH ca vistareNa
   saṃprakāśayata / saṃkṣepānmārṣā yadi tathāgataḥ	saMprakASayata / saMkzepAt mArzAH yadi taTAgataH
   kalpasthitikenāyuḥpramāṇena rātriṃdivamadhitiṣṭhamāno 'sya	kalpa sTiti kena AyuH pramANena rAtriMdivam aDitizWamAnaH asya
   dharmaparyāyasya varṇaṃ bhāṣate, naivāsya dharmaparyāyasya varṇaparyanto	Darma paryAyasya varNam BAzate, na eva asya Darma paryAyasya varNa paryantaH 
   bhavet, na ca tathāgatapratibhānakṣayo bhavet / yathā	Bavet, na ca taTAgata pratiBAna kzayaH Bavet / yaTA
   tathāgataśīlasamādhiprajñāvimuktijñānadarśanamapramāṇamaparyantam, evameva	taTAgata SIla samADi prajQA vimukti jQAna darSanam apramANam aparyantam, evam eva
   mārṣā ya imaṃ dharmaparyāyamudgrahīṣyati dhārayiṣyati vācayiṣyati	mArzAH yaH imam Darma paryAyam udgrahIzyati DArayizyati vAcayizyati
   likhiṣyati likhāpayiṣyati paryavāpsyati pravartayiṣyati, parṣanmadhye ca	liKizyati liKApayizyati paryavApsyati pravartayizyati, parzad maDye ca
   vistareṇa saṃprakāśayiṣyati   anena cittena kathamamī sattvā	vistareNa saMprakASayizyati  anena cittena kaTam amI sattvA
   evamudāradharmasya lābhinaḥ syuriti śraddhayā satkṛtya śrāvayiṣyanti	evam udAra Darmasya lABinaH syuH iti SradDayA satkRtya SrAvayizyanti
   śroṣyanti ca yoniśo manasi bhāvayiṣyanti ca / pustakalikhitaṃ kṛtvā gṛhe	Srozyanti ca yoniSas manasi BAvayizyanti ca / pustaka liKitam kRtvA gRhe
   dhārayiṣyati satkariṣyati gurukariṣyati mānayiṣyati pūjayiṣyati /	DArayizyati satkarizyati gurukarizyati mAnayizyati pUjayizyati /
   amātsaryacittatayā asya dharmaparyāyasya varṇaṃ bhāṣitvā likhanāya	amAtsarya citta tayA asya Darma paryAyasya varNam BAzitvA liKanAya
   vācanāya svādhyayanāya pūjanāya darśanāya dāsyati, teṣāmapi nāsti	vAcanAya svADyayanAya pUjanAya darSanAya dAsyati, tezAm api na asti
   puṇyaparyantaḥ //	puNya paryantaH //
   atha khalu bhagavānasyaiva dharmaparyāyasya bhūyasyā mātrayā	aTa Kalu BagavAn asya eva Darma paryAyasya BUyasyA mAtrayA
   anuparindanārthaṃ tasyāṃ velāyāmimā gāthā abhāṣata  	anuparindana arTam tasyAm velAyAm imAH gATAH aBAzata  
   sattvā dṛṣṭā ye mayā buddhadṛṣṭyā te 'rhantaḥ syuḥ śāriputreṇa tulyāḥ /	sattvAH dRzwAH ye mayA budDa dRzwyA te arhantaH syuH SAriputreNa tulyAH /
   tāṃ cetkaścitpūjayetkalpakoṭyā tulyān gaṅgāvālukābhiryathaiva // 1 //	tAm ced kaScid pUjayet kalpa kowyA tulyAn gaFgA vAlukABiH yaTA eva // 1 //
   pratyekabuddhāya tu yaśca pūjāṃ kuryādahorātramapi prahṛṣṭaḥ /	pratyekabudDAya tu yaH ca pUjAm kuryAt ahorAtram api prahRzwaH /
   mālyaprakāraiśca tathāmbaraiśca tasmādayaṃ puṇyakṛto viśiṣṭaḥ // 2 //	mAlya prakArEH ca taTA ambarEH ca tasmAt ayam puNya kRtaH viSizwaH // 2 //
   sarve 'pi pratyekajinā yadi syustān pūjayet kaścidihāpramattaḥ /	sarve api pratyeka jinAH yadi syuH tAn pUjayet kaScid iha apramattaH /
   (Dbh 110)	(DB 110)
   puṣpaiśca gandhaiśca vilepanaiśca kalpānanekān śayanānnapānaiḥ // 3 //	puzpEH ca ganDEH ca vilepanEH ca kalpAn anekAn Sayana anna pAnEH // 3 //
   ekasya yaścaiva tathāgatasya kuryāt praṇāmamapi caikavāram /	ekasya yaH ca eva taTAgatasya kuryAt praNAmam api ca eka vAram /
   prasannacitto 'tha vadennamo 'rhan tasmādidaṃ śreṣṭhataraṃ ca puṇyam // 4	prasanna cittaH aTa vadet namaH arhan tasmAt idam SrezWataram ca puNyam // 4
   buddhā bhaveyuryadi sarvasattvāstān pūjayet yaśca yathaiva pūrvam /	budDAH BaveyuH yadi sarva sattvAH tAn pUjayet yaH ca yaTA eva pUrvam /
   divyaiśca puṣpairatha mānuṣaiśca kalpānanekān bahubhiḥ prakāraiḥ // 5 //	divyEH ca puzpEH aTa mAnuzEH ca kalpAn anekAn bahuBiH prakArEH // 5 //
   yaścaiva saddharmavilopakāle tyaktvā svakāyaṃ ca tathātmajīvam /	yaH ca eva sat Darma vilopa kAle tyaktvA sva kAyam ca taTA Atma jIvam /
   dadyādahorātramidaṃ hi sūtraṃ viśiṣyate puṇyamidaṃ hi tasmāt // 6 //	dadyAt ahorAtram idam hi sUtram viSizyate puNyam idam hi tasmAt // 6 //
   yasyepsitaṃ pūjayituṃ jinendrān pratyekabuddhānapi śrāvakāṃśca /	yasya Ipsitam pUjayitum jinendrAn pratyekabudDAn api SrAvakAn= ca /
   dṛḍhaṃ samutpādya sa bodhicittam idaṃ sadā sūtravaraṃ dadātu // 7 //	dRXam samutpAdya sa boDi cittam idam sadA sUtra varam dadAtu // 7 //
   rājā hyayaṃ sarvasubhāṣitānāṃ so 'bhudgataḥ sarvatathāgatānāma /	rAjA hi ayam sarva suBAzitAnAm saH aBudgataH sarva taTAgatAnAmaH /
   gṛhe sthitastasya tathāgataḥ sa tiṣṭhedidaṃ yatra hi sūtraratnam // 8 //	gRhe sTitaH tasya taTAgataH sa tizWet idam yatra hi sUtra ratnam // 8 //
   prabhāṃ sa prāpnoti śubhāmanantām ekaṃ padaṃ vādi śatīhayaśca /	praBAm sa prApnoti SuBAm anantAm ekam padam vAdi SatIhayaH ca /
   na vyañjanād grasyati nāpi cārthād dadāti yaḥ sūtramidaṃ parebhyaḥ // 9 //	na vyaQjanAt grasyati na api ca arTAt dadAti yaH sUtram idam pareByaH // 9 //
   anuttarāsau naranāyakānāṃ sattvo na kaścit sadṛśo 'sya vidyate /	anuttarA asO nara nAyakAnAm sattvaH na kaScid sadRSaH asya vidyate /
   bhavetsamudreṇa samaśca so 'kṣayaḥ śrutvā hi yo dharmamimaṃ prapadyate //	Bavet samudreNa samaH ca saH akzayaH SrutvA hi yaH Darmam imam prapadyate //
   According the edition by Ryūkḥ Kondḥ (reproduced Kyoto 1983) the end of	Accordinj Te edition bi RyUkH KondH (reproduced KyotaH 1983) Te end of
   the sūtra is:	Te sUtre is:
   idam avocad bhagavān āttamanās te vimukticandrapūrvaṃgamā bodhisattvagaṇā	idam avocat BagavAn Atta manAH te vimukti candra pUrvaMgamA boDisattva gaNA
   vaśavartidevarājapramukhāḥ sarvadevādhipatīśvarāś ca mahānandapūrvaṃgamā	vaSa varti deva rAja pramuKAH sarva deva aDipati ISvarAH ca mahAnanda pUrvaMgamA
   sarvamahāśrāvakagaṇāḥ sadevamānuṣāsuragandharvaś ca lokaḥ sā sarvāvatī	sarva mahA SrAvaka gaNAH sa deva mAnuza asura ganDarvaH ca lokaH sA sarvAvatI
   parṣad bhagavato vajragarbhasya bhāṣitam abhyanandann iti //	parzad BagavataH vajragarBasya BAzitam aByanandan iti //
   iti parindanāparivarto nāmaikādaśamaḥ //	iti parindanAparivartaH nAma ekAdaSamaH //
   iti śrībodhisattvacaryāprasthāno daśabhūmīśvaro nāma	iti SrI boDisattva caryA prasTAnaH daSa BUm ISvaraH nAma
   mahāyānasūtraratnarājaḥ samāptaḥ //	mahAyAna sUtra ratna rAjaH samAptaH //
   ye dharmā hetuprabhavā hetun teṣāṃ tathāgato hy avadat /	ye DarmAH hetu praBavAH hetun tezAm taTAgataH hi avadat /
   teṣāṃ ca yo nirodho evaṃ vādī mahāśramaṇaḥ //	tezAm ca yaH niroDaH evam vAdI mahA ASramaNaH //
